 All higher education institutions will now conduct entrance examinations, not individual agencies, but an agency, which will be named National Testing (NTA) Agency
 neshnal testing agency kii sthapana kaa faisla shuukravaar kii shaam ko cabinet kii baithak main liya gaya

 The government will appoint its director general and it will also have a board of governors elected from different institutions

 After the establishment, the National Testing Agency will first take the examinations that CBSE currently conducts

 neshnal testing agency kii sthapana ke baad alag-alag pariksha main shaamil hone vaale 40 lakh vidhyaarthiyon ko phayda hoga

 Forced by the situation, Chief Minister Akhilesh left for Deoria from Lucknow in the evening and went to the ancestral village of CO - Nunakhar Juwafar and met family members and announced a CBI inquiry into the murder
 is dauraan unhone peedit parivaar ko 50 lakh rupee aarthik madad, parivaar ke ek sadsy ko sarkari naukari or puure maamle kii sibiai jaanch ke aadesh die
 After receiving assurance from the Chief Minister, Haq's family agreed to perform the last rites
 akhilesh ne kaha ki rajya sarkaar ghatana ko lekar bahut aahat he
 No one will be spared, no matter who they are
 unhone kaha ki agar purv cabinet mantri raghuraaj pratap singh urf raja bhaiya hatyakand main doshi paae gaye to unke khilaaf bhi kathor karwai hogi
 Earlier, the state government suspended three policemen who had escaped leaving them alone on the day of the incident in the CO murder case
 uttar pradesh ke apper police mahanideshak (kanoon evam vyavastha) arun kumaar ne somvaar ko samvaadadaataaon ko bataaya ki kunda kotwali ke prabharee sarvesh mishra, varisht upanireekshak vinay kumaar singh or sio ke ganar imran ko nilambit kar diya gaya he
 It is being investigated that under which circumstances these policemen run away leaving their officer alone on the spot
 tippaniyan Earlier, the state cabinet minister Azam Khan questioned the role of the fleeing policemen leaving Haq alone, stating that the policemen who had fled at the time of the attack were either cowardly or involved in the assassination plot
 aise pulicekarmiyon ko naukari main bane rahane kaa koi adhikaar nahin he
 It is noteworthy that in the incident of firing between two factions in Valipur village of Kunda area late on Saturday, two people including the village head teenager were killed
 ghatana ko niyantrit karne pahunche kunda ke sio jila ul haq kii bhi hinsa ke dauraan bheed dwaara hatya kar di gai thi
 On the complaint of co's wife Parveen Azad, a case was registered against Raja Bhaiya for plotting murder and seven of his supporters were involved in the murder in Pratapgarh
 maamle main ab tak guddu singh or rajeev singh ko giraftaar kiya gaya, jo raja bhaiya ke kareebi bataae ja rahe hai
 Seeing the matter taking hold, Raja Bhaiya met Chief Minister Akhilesh Yadav in Lucknow and submitted his resignation
 unka istipha bhi sweekaar kar liya gaya
 Describing the resignation as inadequate, the opposition parties created a ruckus in the assembly demanding the arrest of Raja Bhaiya
 bahujan samaaj party netaa nasimuddin siddiki ne kaha ki sio kii hatya suniyojit dhang se karai gai
 The Akhilesh government does not have the right to remain in power even for a minute
 istipha dene ke baad raja bhaiya ne sadan ke saath-saath media ko bhi apni safai di
 Raja Bhaiya said in his clarification, "I have nothing to do with the CO murder case
 mujhe sio kii hatya karwaane kii kya jarurat thi agar sio se mujhe koi samasya hoti to main tabadalaa karvaa detaa
 i had a government and i was a minister
 " unhone kaha, "sio kareeb chah maheene se kunda main tainaat the
 He was very good and simple in nature
 mujhe unase koi dikkat nahin thi
 On the contrary, i heard that he himself used to say that no political intervention is done in Kunda
 kaam karne ke liye yah acchhee jagah he
 " raja bhaiya ne kaha, "jo log mujhe mantri pad se hataanaa chaahate the ve kaamyaab ho gaye
 But now by filing a fake case, the real culprits will not be punished
 " After the resignation of Raja Bhaiya, Chief Minister Akhilesh felt that the co's family would agree to the funeral for demanding strict action by sending Director General of Police AC Sharma to Deoria
